#999000name;Winds of Change;;;;;;;;;;X
#999000desc;The political reality in our country has changed, and is time to show the rest of the world proudly.;;;;;;;;;;X
#999000a;For the people;;;;;;;;;;X
#999000b;For the nation;;;;;;;;;;X
#999000c;For our rights;;;;;;;;;;X

# Austalia

event = {
id = 999000
random = no
persistent = yes
country = AST

decision = { 
	OR = {
		AND = {
			NOT = { local_flag = ASTCOM }
		OR = {
			ideology = leninist
			ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = ASTDEM }
		OR = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			ideology = social_liberal
			ideology = market_liberal
			ideology = social_conservative
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = ASTFAS }
		OR = {
			ideology = nazi
			ideology = fascist
			}
		}
	}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		ai = no
	}

trigger = {
ai = yes
OR = {
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = ASTCOM }
		OR = {
			ideology = leninist
			ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = ASTDEM }
		OR = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			ideology = social_liberal
			ideology = market_liberal
			ideology = social_conservative
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = ASTFAS }
		OR = {
			ideology = nazi
			ideology = fascist
			}
		}
	}
}

name = "999000name"
desc = "999000desc"
style = 2

date = { day = 2 month = july year = 1914 }
offset = 1
deathdate = { day = 30 month = december year = 1990 }

action = {
	trigger = { government = communist }

	name = "999000a"

	command = { type = flag_ext where = AST which = "_com" }
	command = { type = name where = AST which = "Australian Republic"}
	command = { type = local_setflag which = ASTCOM }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = ASTFAS }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = ASTDEM }
	}
		
action = {
	trigger = { government = Fascist }

	name = "999000b"

	command = { type = flag_ext where = AST which = "_fas" }
	command = { type = name where = AST which = "Australia"}
	command = { type = local_setflag which = ASTFAS }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = ASTCOM }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = ASTDEM }
	}		
		
action = {
	trigger = { government = Democratic }

	name = "999000c"

	command = { type = flag_ext where = AST which = ""}
	command = { type = name where = AST which = ""}
	command = { type = local_setflag which = ASTDEM }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = ASTCOM }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = ASTFAS }
	}		
} 


#America - North

event = {
id = 999001
random = no
persistent = yes
country = USA

decision = { 
	OR = {
		AND = {
			NOT = { local_flag = USACOM }
		OR = {
			ideology = leninist
			ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = USADEM }
		OR = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			ideology = social_liberal
			ideology = market_liberal
			ideology = social_conservative
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = USAFAS }
		OR = {
			ideology = nazi
			ideology = fascist
			}
		}
	}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		ai = no
	}

trigger = {
ai = yes
OR = {
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = USACOM }
		OR = {
			ideology = leninist
			ideology = stalinist
			}
		}

		OR = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			ideology = social_liberal
			ideology = market_liberal

			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = USAFAS }
		OR = {
			ideology = nazi
			ideology = fascist
			}
		}
	}
}

name = "999000name"
desc = "999000desc"
style = 2

date = { day = 2 month = july year = 1914 }
offset = 1
deathdate = { day = 30 month = december year = 1990 }

action = {
	trigger = { government = communist }

	name = "999000a"

	command = { type = flag_ext where = USA which = "_communist" }
	command = { type = name where = USA which = "United Socialist States of America"}
	command = { type = local_setflag which = USACOM }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = USAFAS }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = USADEM }
	}
		
action = {
	trigger = { government = Fascist }

	name = "999000b"

	command = { type = flag_ext where = USA which = "_nazi" }
	command = { type = name where = USA which = "Unified States of America"}
	command = { type = local_setflag which = USAFAS }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = USACOM }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = USADEM }
	}		
		
action = {
	trigger = { government = Democratic }

	name = "999000c"

	command = { type = flag_ext where = USA }
	command = { type = name where = USA }
	command = { type = local_setflag which = USADEM }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = USACOM }
	command = { type = local_clrflag which = USAFAS }
	}		
}

event = {
id = 999080
random = no
persistent = yes
country = NAM

decision = { 
	OR = {
		AND = {
			NOT = { local_flag = NAMCOM }
		OR = {
			ideology = leninist
			ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = NAMDEM }
		OR = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			ideology = social_liberal
			ideology = market_liberal
			ideology = social_conservative
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = NAMFAS }
		OR = {
			ideology = nazi
			ideology = fascist
			}
		}
	}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		ai = no
	}

trigger = {
ai = yes
OR = {
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = NAMCOM }
		OR = {
			ideology = leninist
			ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = NAMDEM }
		OR = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			ideology = social_liberal
			ideology = market_liberal
			ideology = social_conservative
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = NAMFAS }
		OR = {
			ideology = nazi
			ideology = fascist
			}
		}
	}
}

persistent = yes
tag = { FIN U20 }

decision = { 
	OR = {
		AND = {
			NOT = { local_flag = FINCOM }
		OR = {
			ideology = leninist
			ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = FINDEM }
		OR = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			ideology = social_liberal
			ideology = market_liberal
			ideology = social_conservative
			}
		}
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = FINFAS }
		OR = {
			ideology = nazi
			ideology = fascist
			}
		}
	}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		ai = no
	}

trigger = {
ai = yes
OR = {
	AND = {
		NOT = { local_flag = FINCOM }
		OR = {
			ideology = leninist
			ideology = stalinist
			}
		}

		OR = {

		}

			}
		}
	}
}
